msg:The hotel is in a very good location, on the edge of the West Lake, next to Shangri-La and Xinxin, with a large garden inside, divided into several buildings. We stayed in a room along the street in Building 5. The room was not big, the toilet was a little crowded, the toilet was inductive, it could be cleaned and flushed, and it flushed automatically. The washbasin had direct drinking water and automatic hand sanitizer, but it was a little small. The bathroom was a shower. The glass separating the toilet shower and the room could be set to a frosted effect. Compared with the toilet, the room equipment was a little old. A lot of water, fruit, and drinks were sent to the room. The bed was very comfortable, with the right softness and hardness. However, the bedside socket was a little old, and there was no type c socket, which could actually be ignored. The main disadvantage was that the room was not soundproof. When we came back from the opposite room in the middle of the night, the sound was loud and woke us up. The sound of cars passing by on the road outside was not that noisy. The service was OK, and they helped us delay check-out until 2 o'clock, which was very satisfactory. Another point is that the breakfast was rich in variety, including cakes, pastries, and bread, which were high-end goods at a glance, not comparable to ordinary hotels. The food was quite satisfactory, and the restaurant layout was quite stylish, which enhanced the overall sense of value. The sound insulation can really be improved during the next renovation, otherwise it will affect the overall experience.

name:J‚Äçu‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçz‚Äçh‚Äçe
info:Standard King Bed Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:4.7
posted:Posted January 5, 2024
msg:West Lake Villa is located on the bank of West Lake. It is built along the mountain slope and blends in with the West Lake landscape. The mountains and lakes are dependent on each other. The villa is full of greenery and picturesque scenery. Outside the villa, Su Causeway faces each other, Bai Causeway overlooks, isolated islands depend on each other, and Yue Temple is adjacent. West Lake Villa makes full use of the original ecological landscape characteristics of the site, creating scenery according to the situation, garden setting and culture as the scenery, creating the characteristics of "secretness, lushness, elegance and appreciation". The buildings of the villa cannot be seen from the outside. When you enter the villa, there are lush trees and elegant scenery. The six buildings depend on each other to form a beautiful picture. Entering each building, you can feel the spaciousness and grandeur of each building, which is difficult to achieve in ordinary hotels. You can use battery cars to go to various buildings, and you can also roam freely to enjoy the beautiful scenery in the courtyard.
During the G20 Summit in Hangzhou, West Lake Villa was selected as a dedicated hotel to receive domestic and foreign guests. There is an old building in the hotel called the "May 4th Constitution Historical Materials Exhibition Hall", which was the place where the first Constitution of New China was drafted in 1954. In December 1953, Chairman Mao led a constitution drafting team to Hangzhou, and its office was located where the May 4th Constitution Historical Materials Exhibition Hall is today. When I first saw the May 4th Constitution, I thought it had something to do with the May 4th Movement. After a closer look, I discovered that it was China‚Äôs first constitution in 1954. Make no mistake! !
The facilities in the hotel are very modern. The curtains have electric switches, the bathtub curtains can automatically set atomization, and the bathrooms are all smart toilets. What needs to be mentioned is that the flowers indoors are real flowers, not plastic flowers. At first I thought they were plastic flowers when I saw such blooming flowers!
The drinks in the refrigerator are free, and snacks with local Hangzhou characteristics are delivered every day (I don‚Äôt know if it‚Äôs a New Year‚Äôs Day discount). Maybe everyone is concerned about whether there is a parking lot if you drive by yourself? You can park in front of each building. If you can't park, there is a special underground parking lot. If it is an electric vehicle, you can use the charging pile to charge your Baoju. Parking is free for hotel guests. The hotel's restaurant is very a**ospheric, with a variety of meals to choose from. Mainly Chinese style, supplemented by Western style. You can experience a lot of authentic Hangzhou cuisine here. It is worth mentioning that there is actually natural honeycomb honey that can be eaten. The honeycomb honey hanging on the shelf is very spectacular!
The very, very important reason I like it here is the tranquility. Although the West Lake is outside, and people come and go during New Year's Day, and there is a constant flow of people on the street until midnight, but it is quiet inside the hotel courtyard, undisturbed by the noise outside. It can be quiet or noisy, switch as you like.

     The hotel is backed by Baoshi Mountain, and the whole is a big park. Several small buildings are built on the mountain, among them, our room is in Building 5 where the main station is located. The room is quite satisfactory, with electric curtains, smart toilet, and Dyson hair dryer. The shower room is too simple, and there is no place for personal bathing items, which is a little lacking.
    The breakfast restaurant is in Building 1, and there is a shuttle bus in the hotel. The breakfast is really good. In addition to the regular porridge, noodles, pastry, etc., there are also local specialties and Japanese meals. All kinds of flavors are considered. The sweet-scented osmanthus lotus root powder is very fragrant and thick, which goes well with the natural honey next to it. There are many kinds of milk, as well as goat milk. There is nothing to say about the dining environment. There are a few red plums and early cherry blossoms in front of the window, reflecting the morning sun, which is cozy and beautiful.
     After the meal, we took a stroll in the hotel garden. It was quiet and peaceful. Several red plants were in full bloom, and the fragrance was refreshing. There is the former site where the May Fourth Constitution was drafted in the hotel. It is very commemorative to bring the baby to check in. In Chairman Mao‚Äôs residence, the oversized desk is full of books, and there are even books in front of the bathtub. Sure enough, Grandpa Mao loved reading.
     The Lixi Lake of the West Lake is just outside the hotel, and the Broken Bridge and Xiaogu Mountain are not far away. There are many people doing morning exercises in the morning. My husband went out for a run in the morning and was very satisfied. Take a leisurely walk on Beishan Road in the evening, leaning on the railing on the second floor of the Starbucks where Jiang Jingguo lived: Lei Feng Tower and Chenghuang Pavilion complement each other, the West Lake is shimmering, the Broken Bridge is full of tourists, and the Nanshan Mountains are picturesque.
     The beautiful scenery of West Lake is different in four seasons. Waiting to experience it quietly, next time I come to Hangzhou, I will choose West Lake Villa.

The scenery of Beishan Street is very good, it is during the Spring Festival There are a lot of people, and it takes half an hour to drive from the intersection of Beishan Street to the hotel.

Facilities: The lobby is at the southeast gate, and the restaurant is in Building 1. Some of the rooms are in Building 3 and some are in Building 6. There is a park along the way, and the scenery is very good and quiet. The room is not big, but the hardware is advanced, electric curtains, charging and switching lights are very smart and convenient, and the toilet is a sensory smart toilet seat.
Disadvantages: The countertop in the bathroom is small, and there is no separate exhaust facility in the bathroom, so there will be a peculiar smell when you open the door of the area where the toilet is located. The air conditioner is good for heating, but the noise of the internal unit is loud. However, if you turn on the heating all day during the day, you don‚Äôt need to turn on the air conditioner at night, and the room insulation effect is very good.

Hygiene: The ground is the floor and it is cleaned very cleanly.

Service: The villa is relatively large, you can call a battery car to pick it up, and the takeaway will also be delivered to the room. The service attitude is very good.

Breakfast: The buffet is rich, the taste is good, and the fruits are very fresh.
